<text>Brother picked up the food from here for dinner. So I didn't know why to expect.  Strictly reviewing the food, it's not bad.  We got the party platter with chicken and beef shwarma, with fries and basmati rice. ($35). We also ordered a chicken kabob plate ($13) with pita, Cesar salad and basmati rice. Extra pita pita bread about $.75 per order and baklava about $5.

All the flavors were on point, but the meats this batch was just a tad dry. Fries were a bit overcooked as well, but I'm sure if it was due to the container and the time from pick up to delivery.  The garlic sauce was excellent, creamy with bold garlic flavor and they gave plenty of it.

Personally, I feel the food would be much better when eaten fresh off the grill and not with the travel time.  Or  maybe if some steam was allowed to escape from the container so food doesn't continue to cook. Who knows?

I would return here because it's convenient and give it one more try.< /text><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM0e8OJAvdf0jdI1jONu2aBLJdkB4j7YCie7548=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP2tG21BIvnAe7lQoaZoRmKFdoCr1PUKNEDSqK3=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOuyYGXfyJcU2O7YsfbrkN6maLpfH06p6IzTLE9=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM39hoR5XL6oV4BQjjI5xfo2vvDxZM3D3Tvmn9y=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipND3HypjcztThHfcAQJRV5aMu2BJHrSvDCFSjfN=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMJjBCwLX7y5_KYz0ttlTwVlQEGb1OePD1p3Wfr=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</Pictures>< Resp>

I remove a star for every major issue I encounter with a business. I've never been to the facility myself but I found it as a place for my husband to take our 2 boys for treatment. The first issue is being able to get through. It was so hard to do which should've been a sign but I admit I chose to ignore it and was able to get through after 12 attempts of getting the busy signal (they really need to have additional lines for business). We scheduled their exams and was provided treatment suggestions for the both of them. Now I will say this, Dr. Audrey, I will be grateful for confirming my suspicion of my youngest son having problems with breathing and putting a name to that. He's since had a successful tonsillectomy and adenoidectomy and doing better than ever thanks to your referral. However, the dental work that both of my boys needed were supposed to be requested with the dental insurance company so we can anticipate our share of cost and set everything up for the work to be done. And that was the 2nd issue. After countless times of reaching out to the office about scheduling and determining what our cost share would be, each time the staff says the same thing: "um we haven't reached out yet, do you want to just have it done and then we tell you how much it'll cost in the form of a bill or do you want to reschedule?" Excuse me? Yeah let me just have the services done so you can send me a huge bill and demand it in full or by a certain date or it'll go to collections. What if it's a ridiculous amount and I'd rather save to have it paid in full prior to having it done? And reschedule? Yeah cause I have so many dates available that I can just easily call off from work. I mean it's unbelievable how inconsiderate they are!! I just thank God we've found a place that's better, easier to work with and get through on the first try. I do NOT recommend this place, it will truly be a waste of your time. Remember your dental insurance only covers for the first exam of the year. Make sure it's with a dental office that takes your treatment seriously and will follow up with you!< /Text>

<date>1560281418973< /date>< rate>

<text>I was really skeptical about trying Cauldron because I had a bad experience with nitrogen ice cream @ a different shop in Monrovia but I'm so glad I gave this place a go.  I was a fan from the first taste.

I know that some people get thrown off by the texture of nitrogen ice cream because of how thick it can be but Cauldron was pretty smooth. I've tried several different flavors but Sun, Moon & Stars is hands-down my favorite.  It didn't take too long to make yet it was really cold.  Cold enough not to melt inside a hot, freshly made Hong Kong waffle (they call it their "puffle cone").

Service is okay.  There is only one bench to sit on inside with some table seating right outside the shop and plenty of public seating in the shared space of nice Asian plaza in which they're located.

Aesthetics: 4/5
Service: 3/5
Food: 4/5
Recommend: YES<//text>< pics>

<user>114163245199762787895< /user><user_name>Grace Lieu</user_name><Date>1543291251150< /Date>< Rate>
4< /Rate>
< review>
Family and I went to their grand opening a month ago and ordered the Sun, Moon, and Stars ice cream with a red velvet puffle cone (essentially a Hong Kong egg waffle) and just a Family size (4 scoops) cup of the Earl Grey Lavender. Waiting for the ice cream wasn't long even though it's made to order. All of them were pretty good and I also like that they can make the ice cream into a rose shape! The only thing I didn't like was the fact that you could only get 1 flavor for the 4 scoops instead of individual flavors, but I understand that it's not pre-made and it'd take longer to make 4 different flavors. Also, it's pricey too but the ice cream is made with nitrogen, making it more creamy and denser, so probably that's why. Overall, a pretty solid ice cream place!<//review>

Oh boy, was my experience here bad. We came with a party of 5, and were seated at the only table large enough to fit us all, at the very back of the restaurant. There was only one other party in the entire building, an old couple enjoying lunch. The only waitress in sight acted like it was her first day on the job. We ordered calamari as an appetizer, and after waiting an unnessecarily long amount of time, we recieved fish sticks and ranch. We complained to the waitress, and she came back with, "Oh, we have a new cook, he's still learning." At that point I was ready to leave, but the rest of my party wasn't. I ordered a simple cheeseburger thinking that they couldn't screw it up. The bun ended up being stale and burned, and the meat tasted like it was meant to be thrown away. We paid and walked out as quickly as possible.</review>

I was hopeful due to all the high reviews of thos placr, and on approach it looked exactly like a placed my girlfriend and i would enjoy. For the most part it was ok in the beginning but the longer we stayed the mote dissapointed we became.

Service was mediocre, and after had found out we were being served by the manager it was a little more disappointing.

The bathrooms had not been serviced.

The atmosphere had a lot of potential. Thr place looks nice. But that was kind of ruined by the type of clientele they bring in. At least while we were there we had felt less like we were in a family restaurant and more like a dive bar with a couple of drunk patrons at the bar acting like this was just tbat, a bar, and not a place for someone to get a decent and quiet meal.

The food that we found edible was good. Nithing to write home about but not bad in any respect. Except that our order of chicken tenders was dangerously undercooked, so we had that taken off our meal which at least the manager was polite enough not to deny.

All in all i had high hopes from what we saw walking up, but on this day, it seemes that nothing was really worth the trip.

Bases on my experience I would not return, nor would suggest this location.< /review>

< text>
Re; Saturday evening 6/17/17 - I have been going to Castle Rock Restaurant for a long time, mainly to listen and dance to the music of the fantastic duo band, Take Two. But also for the fantastic service of the waitress, Sonia, and the good Manhattans and great steak salad. The new management still kept the great steak salad, and Take Two remains terrific, but the new management let go the best waitress imaginable, Sonia, and despite the knowledge that a large crowd would be there last night for Take Two, they only had ONE waitress, the new and overwhelmed, Cynthia, and ONE bartender. We waited over an hour and a half before we could even place our drink and dinner order. If it wasn't for Take Two, we would have left. I sure hope they bring back Sonia, or we will eat and drink elsewhere  before coming for the band.
UPDATE 6/25/17 (Sunday evening) - Castle Rock had sufficient wait staff this time for the crowd that comes for the fabulous music of Take Two. They even had table cloths on all the tables. The Manhattans were fine. But unfortunately they really skimped on what used to be a fabulous steak salad. I will go back because of the band and the improved service. Really disappointed by the just OK steak salad (which used to be the best I ever had anywhere). Guess they also changed chefs.
UPDATE 7/22/17 (Saturday evening). OK. The management is listening. We returned for the once-a-month Saturday music of the really fun band, Take Two, and although the crowd was much less than last month (when the service was incredibly awful and inadequate),  at least there was  now adequate wait staff to service us in a timely manner. Nick, a now experienced waiter and his waiter-in-training, Tyler, did a good job. And the quality of the steak salad has come back. We will come back. :-)
UPDATE 7/23/17 (Sunday evening) - I was accosted on the dance floor and then threatened by the owner of the  Castle Rock building that if I didn't stop (I'm assuming someone identified me to her as the writer of these reviews) she would no longer host the band. This was after I had been served a warm Manhattan, which I was just going to let go.  Apparently the owner of the business, the restaurant and bar, was also present.  I later learned one of the owners berated another paying customer for going in search of her dinner, which was taking so long to be delivered. By the way, the only diners in the restaurant that I observed were the dancers, at Castle Rock solely because the band was there. Without the great band, Take Two, there would have been like 40 less dinners sold that evening. And by the way, the average age of us dancers is probably 72. I can't imagine what the owner of the building and the owner of the business were thinking when they berated their elderly customers.<//text>

After 51 years of living with crooked teeth, my employer added adult ortho to our dental plan and it was time to correct. I was referred by my dentist to Montano Elevated Orthodontics. I am so glad they did. I never realized before the correction just HOW crooked and how much my teeth affected my appearance. < review>
I went to Montano and Cardall orthodontics after receiving a recommendation from my dentist. I had always been unhappy with my smile and thought it was finally time to take care of it. After getting some surprising news that my case was going to be more in depth than the typical orthodontic case, I wasn‚Äôt sure what to do. I was informed along with braces I would also need to undergo two surgeries. This news was not fun to hear but I knew I needed to proceed. I never felt the need to get a second opinion because Dr. Montano and the staff made me feel comfortable and secure that my well being was in great hands. They were very quick to get started and on my way to a perfect smile. 3 months after getting my braces I had my first surgery. That experience was a game changer. The procedure is known as SARPE (surgically assisted rapid palatal expansion) and I‚Äôm not going to sugar coat it, it SUCKED! I was unable to chew anything for 2 months, causing me to lose 25 pounds, it left me with a inch gap in between my two front teeth, and I also had a large very uncomfortable metal device attached to my top teeth holding my jaw together. Needless to say for about 10 months (the total time it took to completely heal) I was immensely regretting my decision. This also led me to have a conversation with Dr. Montano about my apprehension to proceed with the next, more invasive, surgery. But luck was fortunately on my side! Dr. Montano felt the results from my first surgery were better than expected and I would be able to get away without having to do the second procedure. This was amazing news for me to hear and brightened my spirits.
So after 2 years and 3 months and one horrible surgical experience I am happy to say my braces are now off and I am happier than ever. My road to a beautiful smile would not be the same without everyone at the Montano and Cardall office. I cannot speak highly enough of all of them. Dr. Montano and Dr. Cardall were incredible at making me feel that my case was important and it was their mission to provide me with the best care. Every one of the assistants are caring and sympathetic. They took special care of me and I am forever grateful. Anyone who is unhappy with their smile should definitely go see Montano and Cardall orthodontic specialists! It will change your life.</review>

< Review>
I had a wonderful experience working with Dr. Montano and Dr. Cardall's team.

When I relocated from Washington State 2 years ago, I was wearing bonded brackets and not sure if I wanted to switch to Invisalign.  Dr. Montano facilitated my decision making which resulted in decreased frequency dental decay and abscesses because wearing Invisalign facilitated my oral hygiene, aside being pain free from mouth sores due to the oral contact with wires/hooks and brackets.

I find every member of the team very supportive and professional throughout my 2 year treatment period.

From Dr. Montano's facial /verbal expression and demeanor, I can tell that Orthodontics is not just a profession but also his passion as well.  He took his time and gave an artistic touch during my treatment.

I'm glad Dr. Caldall joined the team recently so more people in the area can have more chance to shine with their smile.

Thank you all for the fabulous job you are doing for the community!

Ming Chen, MD</Review>
